###########################
####Coup Country Events####
###########################
add_namespace = ron_coupscountry

# May Overthrow
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.1
	title = ron_coupscountry.1.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_early_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ser_may_overthrow
		}
		original_tag = SER
		date > 1903.6.10
		date < 1904.6.10
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Peter I"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = ser_may_overthrow
		news_event = {
			id = ron_early_wars_news.21
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Peter I"
			picture = "WW1/Portrait_Serbia_Peter_I.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
			traits = {
				stout_defender
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = SER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Peter I"
						picture = "WW1/Portrait_Serbia_Peter_I.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							stout_defender
						}
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.2
	title = ron_coupscountry.2.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_early_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = venezuela_coup_1908
		}
		original_tag = VEN
		date > 1908.12.19
		date < 1909.12.19
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Juan Vicente Gomez"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = venezuela_coup_1908
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Juan Vicente Gomez"
			desc = "POLITICS_JUAN_VICENTE_GOMEZ_DESC"
			picture = "WW1/Portrait_Venezuela_Juan_Vicente_Gomez.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = militarism
			traits = {
				dictator
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = VEN
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Juan Vicente Gomez"
						desc = "POLITICS_JUAN_VICENTE_GOMEZ_DESC"
						picture = "WW1/Portrait_Venezuela_Juan_Vicente_Gomez.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = militarism
						traits = {
							dictator
						}
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Goudi Coup
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.3
	title = ron_coupscountry.3.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_early_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = greek_coup_1909
		}
		original_tag = GRE
		date > 1909.8.28
		date < 1910.8.28
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Eleftherios Venizelos"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = greek_coup_1909
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Eleftherios Venizelos"
			picture = "DNC/Eleftherios_Venizelos.dds"
			expire = "1936.3.18"
			ideology = republicanism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GRE
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Eleftherios Venizelos"
						picture = "DNC/Eleftherios_Venizelos.dds"
						expire = "1936.3.18"
						ideology = republicanism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Yuan Shikai Proclaims Himself Emperor
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.6
	title = ron_coupscountry.6.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_early_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = chinese_empire_1916
		}
		original_tag = CHI
		date > 1915.12.12
		date < 1916.12.12
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Yuan Shikai"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = chinese_empire_1916
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Yuan Shikai"
			picture = "WW1/Portrait_China_Yuan_Shikai.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_EOC
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {

					limit = {

						has_government = neutrality

						name = "Yuan Shikai"

			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Costa Rican Coup
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.7
	title = ron_coupscountry.7.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_early_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = costa_rican_coup
		}
		original_tag = COS
		date > 1917.1.27
		date < 1918.1.27
		NOT = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = costa_rican_coup
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			last_election = "1910.1.1"
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			neutrality = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
					only_own_territory = no
					capital = 316
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Kapp Putsch
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.10
	title = ron_coupscountry.10.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Kapp_Putsch
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = kapp_putsch_1920
		}
		original_tag = GER
		date > 1920.3.13
		date < 1921.3.13
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Wolfgang Kapp"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = kapp_putsch_1920
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				last_election = "1920.3.13"
				election_frequency = 60
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 20
				fascism = 60
				communism = 20
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Wolfgang Kapp"
			picture = "INT/Wolfgang_Kapp.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = ultranationalism
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = GEE
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.10.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			news_event = {
				id = ron_coupnews.6
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ruling_party = ROOT
						ideology = fascism
						size = 0.5
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = GER
							has_government = fascism
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Wolfgang Kapp"
							picture = "WW1/Wolfgang_Kapp.dds"
							expire = "2060.1.1"
							ideology = ultranationalism
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = GEE
					}
				}
				50 = {
					news_event = {
						id = ron_coupnews.6
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Reza Khan Seizes Power in Iran
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.11
	title = ron_coupscountry.11.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_early_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = reza_khan_coup_1921
		}
		original_tag = PER
		date > 1921.2.21
		date < 1922.2.21
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {

country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.16
	title = ron_coupscountry.16.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Beer_Hall_Putsch
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = beer_hall_putsch_1920
		}
		original_tag = GER
		date > 1923.11.8
		date < 1924.11.8
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = neutrality
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = beer_hall_putsch_1920
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			last_election = "1923.11.8"
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 20
			fascism = 60
			communism = 20
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Adolf Hitler"
			desc = "POLITICS_ADOLF_HITLER_DESC"
			picture = "INT/Germany_Adolf_Hitler_1923.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = nazism
			traits = {
				GER_hitler_T1
				GER_hitler_T2
				GER_hitler_T3
				GER_hitler_T4
				GER_hitler_T5
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			news_event = {
				id = ron_coupnews.6
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ruling_party = ROOT
						ideology = fascism
						size = 0.5
						only_own_territory = no
						capital = 1105
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = GER
							has_government = fascism
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Adolf Hitler"
							desc = "POLITICS_ADOLF_HITLER_DESC"
							picture = "INT/Germany_Adolf_Hitler_1923.dds"
							expire = "2060.1.1"
							ideology = nazism
							traits = {
								GER_hitler_T1
								GER_hitler_T2
								GER_hitler_T3
								GER_hitler_T4
								GER_hitler_T5
							}
						}
					}
				}
				50 = {
					news_event = {
						id = ron_coupnews.6
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Businessman Plot
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.34
	title = ron_coupscountry.34.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.34.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Business_Plot_1933
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = businessman_plot
		}
		original_tag = USA
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1934.1.1
		has_government = democratic
	}
	immediate = {
		add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = businessman_plot
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.34.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			last_election = "1933.1.1"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			neutrality = 100
		}
		recruit_character = USA_smedley_butler
		USA_smedley_butler = {
			promote_character = {
				Ideology = militarism
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ruling_party = ROOT
						ideology = democratic
						size = 0.4
						only_own_territory = no
						capital = 361
					}
				}
				60 = {
					news_event = {
						id = ron_coupnews.1
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			news_event = {
				id = ron_coupnews.1
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.34.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			news_event = {
				id = ron_coupnews.6
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ruling_party = ROOT
						ideology = neutrality
						size = 0.3
						only_own_territory = no
						capital = 361
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = USA
							has_government = neutrality
						}
						recruit_character = USA_smedley_butler
						USA_smedley_butler = {
							promote_character = {
								Ideology = militarism
							}
						}
					}
				}
				90 = {
					news_event = {
						id = ron_coupnews.6
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		}

		}

		}
		has_government = fascism
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Adolf Hitler"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = germany_coup_1944
	}

			}
		}

		add_stability = -0.1

			name = "Heinrich Himmler"

			ideology = esoteric_nazism
		}
		create_country_leader = {

			ideology = nationalism
		}

			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			neutrality = 60
			democratic = 20
			fascism = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ruling_party = neutrality

							name = "Heinrich Himmler"
							picture = "Portrait_Germany_Heinrich_Himmler.dds"
							expire = "2060.1.1"
							ideology = esoteric_nazism
						}
					}
				}
				70 = {
					news_event = {
						id = ron_coupnews.1
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			news_event = {
				id = ron_coupnews.1
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}

# King Michael's Coup
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.50
	title = ron_coupscountry.50.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Romania_Coup_1944
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = romania_coup_1944
		}
		original_tag = ROM
		date > 1944.7.23
		date < 1944.12.31
		is_in_faction_with = GER
		surrender_progress > 0.1
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = ENG
				has_war_with = USA
			}
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		any_enemy_country = {
			controls_state = 78
		}
		SOV = {
			controls_state = 217
		}
		SOV = {
			controls_state = 219
		}
		SOV = {
			controls_state = 195
		}
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = romania_coup_1944
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.50.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					has_war_with = ROM
				}
				white_peace = ROM
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					has_war_with = ROM
				}
				white_peace = ROM
			}
		}
		GER = {
			end_puppet = ROM
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		SOV = {
			add_to_faction = ROM
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.16
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "King Michael"
			picture = "King_Michael.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			last_election = "1944.7.20"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			neutrality = 60
			communism = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						ideology = fascism
						size = 0.3
						only_own_territory = no
						capital = 46
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROM
							has_government = fascism
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Ion Antonescu"
							desc = "POLITICS_ION_ANTONESCU_DESC"
							picture = "Portrait_Romania_Ion_Antonescu.dds"
							expire = "2060.1.1"
							ideology = legionnairism
							traits = {
								dictator
							}
						}
					}
				}
				70 = {
					news_event = {
						id = ron_coupnews.1
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			news_event = {
				id = ron_coupnews.1
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.50.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			30 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.3
					only_own_territory = no
					capital = 46
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROM
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "King Michael"
						picture = "King_Michael.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
					}
					SOV = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					SOV = {
						country_event = {
							id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.16
							hours = 6
						}
					}
				}
			}
			70 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

# Operation Panzerfaust
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.52
	title = ron_coupscountry.52.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.52.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Operation_Panzerfaust
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = operation_panzerfaust
		}
		original_tag = GER
		date > 1944.9.15
		date < 1944.12.31
		is_in_faction_with = HUN
		NOT = {
			HUN = {
				is_subject_of = GER
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		OR = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				controls_state = 46
			}
			any_enemy_country = {
				controls_state = 48
			}
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = ENG
				has_war_with = USA
			}
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		SOV = {
			controls_state = 217
		}
		SOV = {
			controls_state = 219
		}
		SOV = {
			controls_state = 195
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = operation_panzerfaust
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.52.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		GER = {
			puppet = HUN
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					HUN = {
						start_civil_war = {
							ruling_party = fascism
							ideology = neutrality
							size = 0.5
							only_own_territory = no
							capital = 43
						}
						random_other_country = {
							limit = {

									anti_communist
								}

							SOV = {

							ideology = christian_fascism

							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}

							id = ron_coupnews.1
							hours = 6
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			HUN = {
				add_stability = -0.1
				promote_character = {
					character = HUN_ferenc_szalasi
					ideology = christian_fascism
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					last_election = "1944.1.1"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 100
				}
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.1
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.52.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				every_country = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = SOV
							has_war_with = HUN
						}

				}

						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = ENG

				}

	trigger = {

			has_country_flag = venezuela_coup_1945
		}
		original_tag = VEN
		date > 1945.10.18
		date < 1946.10.18
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Romulo Betancourt"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = venezuela_coup_1945
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1945.1.1"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = democratic
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Romulo Betancourt"
			picture = "CW/Venezuala_RomuloBetancourt.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = socialism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = democratic
					size = 0.5
					only_own_territory = no
					capital = 307
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = VEN
						has_government = democratic
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Romulo Betancourt"
						picture = "CW/Venezuala_RomuloBetancourt.dds"

					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.57
	title = ron_coupscountry.57.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.57.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = hungary_coup_1947
		}
		original_tag = HUN
		date > 1947.5.1
		date < 1948.5.1
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		OR = {
			GER = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			GER = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = GER
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = hungary_coup_1947
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				last_election = "1949.1.1"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				communism = 82
				democratic = 18
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = communism
		promote_character = {
			character = HUN_matyas_rakosi
			ideology = stalinism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}

			50 = {

						original_tag = HUN
						has_government = communism
					}
					promote_character = {
						character = HUN_matyas_rakosi
						ideology = stalinism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}

					}

# 1953 Persia Coup
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.64
	title = ron_coupscountry.64.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.64.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = persia_coup_1953
		}
		original_tag = PER
		date > 1953.8.15
		date < 1953.8.15
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Mohammad Reza Pahlavi"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = persia_coup_1953
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				last_election = "1945.1.1"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mohammad Reza Pahlavi"
			picture = "CW/Iran_Mohammad_Reza_Pahlavi.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = PER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Mohammad Reza Pahlavi"
						picture = "CW/Iran_Mohammad_Reza_Pahlavi.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 14 July Revolution
country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.73
	title = ron_coupscountry.73.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.73.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = iraq_coup_1958
		}
		original_tag = IRQ
		date > 1958.7.14
		date < 1959.7.14
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Abdul Al-Karim Qasim"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = iraq_coup_1958
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Abdul Al-Karim Qasim"
			picture = "CW/Abd_al_Karim_Qasim.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = militarism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = IRQ
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Abdul Al-Karim Qasim"
						picture = "CW/Abd_al_Karim_Qasim.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = militarism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		date < 1959.5.13
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Charles de Gaulle"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}

			}

					hours = 6
				}

		}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = ron_coupscountry.77.a
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.77.b
	}

	id = ron_coupscountry.97
	title = ron_coupscountry.97.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.97.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Bokassa_Coronation
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = bokassa_coronation
		}
		original_tag = CAR
		date > 1977.12.4
		date < 1978.12.4
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Jean-Bédel Bokassa"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_government = neutrality
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = bokassa_coronation
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.97.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			fascism = 100
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "David Dacko"
			picture = "CW/Central_African_Republic_David_Dacko.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = republicanism
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Bokassa I"
			picture = "CW/Emperor_Bokassa.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = nationalist_monarchism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.8
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.97.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.101
	title = ron_coupscountry.101.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = nigeria_coup_1966
		}
		original_tag = NGA
		date > 1966.1.15
		date < 1967.1.15
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Johnson Aguiyi-Ironsi"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = nigeria_coup_1966
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Johnson Aguiyi-Ironsi"
			picture = "CW/NGA_Johnson_Aguiyi-Ironsi.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = militarism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5

				}
			}
			50 = {

					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}

			has_country_flag = iraq_coup_1968
		}
		original_tag = IRQ
		date > 1968.7.17
		date < 1969.7.17
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Ahmed Hassan Al-Bakr"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = iraq_coup_1968
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				fascism = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = fascism
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ahmed Hassan Al-Bakr"
			picture = "CW/Iraq_AhmedHassanAl-Bakr.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = baathism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = fascism
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = IRQ
						has_government = fascism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Ahmed Hassan Al-Bakr"
						picture = "CW/Iraq_AhmedHassanAl-Bakr.dds"

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = syria_coup_1970
		}
		original_tag = SYR
		date > 1970.11.13
		date < 1971.11.13
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Hafez Al-Assad"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = syria_coup_1970
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				fascism = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = fascism
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Hafez Al-Assad"
			picture = "CW/SYR_Hafez_al-Assad.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = baathism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = fascism
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = SYR
						has_government = fascism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Hafez Al-Assad"
						picture = "CW/SYR_Hafez_al-Assad.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = baathism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.120
	title = ron_coupscountry.120.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.120.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = oman_coup_1970
		}
		original_tag = OMA
		date > 1970.7.23
		date < 1971.7.23
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Qaboos Bin Said Al Said"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = oman_coup_1970
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = islamism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = islamism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				islamism = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = islamism
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Qaboos Bin Said Al Said"

			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = emiratism
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Qaboos Bin Said Al Said"
			picture = "CW/Oman_QaboosBinSaidAlSaid.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = islamism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}

			50 = {

					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = islamism
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = OMA
						has_government = islamism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Qaboos Bin Said Al Said"
						picture = "CW/Oman_QaboosBinSaidAlSaid.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = emiratism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Qaboos Bin Said Al Said"
						picture = "CW/Oman_QaboosBinSaidAlSaid.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ron_coupscountry.128.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = dahomey_coup_1972
		}
		original_tag = DAH
		date > 1972.10.26
		date < 1973.10.26
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Mathieu Kerekou"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = dahomey_coup_1972
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				communism = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = communism
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mathieu Kerekou"
			picture = "CW/Benin_Mathieu_Kerekou.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = leninism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

country_event = {

	title = ron_coupscountry.137.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.137.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = bangladesh_coup_1975
		}
		original_tag = BAN
		date > 1975.8.15
		date < 1976.8.15
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Khondaker Mostaq Ahmad"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = bangladesh_coup_1975
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = islamism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = islamism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				islamism = 100

			name = "Khondaker Mostaq Ahmad"

			expire = "2060.1.1"

		}

			hours = 6
		}

				has_government = islamism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

country_event = {
	id = ron_coupscountry.146
	title = ron_coupscountry.146.t
	desc = ron_coupscountry.146.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_modern_coup
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = seychelles_coup_1977
		}
		original_tag = SEY
		date > 1977.6.4
		date < 1978.6.4
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Albert René"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 }
		set_country_flag = seychelles_coup_1977
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = democratic
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Albert René"
			picture = "MD/Seychelles_France-Albert_René.dds"
			ideology = democratic_socialism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = ron_coupnews.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

				factor = 0

			}

		set_country_flag = ECU_coup_2000

		}

					has_government = neutrality
				}

		}

		}
